English

Since the perfect enjoyment of the svar┼лpa of Bhagav─Бn
happens only after reaching a most delightful region
far superior to all others,
that region is also called Paramapada.

muy superior a todos los dem├бs,

which is the recipient of this joy in the attainment of Bhagav─Бn
which is also among the glorious possessions (Vibh┼лtis) of the Lord
and which has, for its attributes, j├▒─Бna and ─Бnanda,
is also (sometimes ) called Paramapada.

que es el receptor de esta alegr├нa en el logro de Bhagav─Бn

y que tiene, por sus atributos, j├▒─Бna y ─Бnanda,
Tambi├йn se llama (a veces) Paramapada.

What appears disagreeable to the man suffering from (excess of) bile
is felt as agreeable when the bile has decreased.

English

Again when the prince is in the prison house it is disagreeable.
But when the emperor is pleased to set him free
and to place him by his own side to enjoy like-pleasures,
the prison house may appear agreeable
as a symbol of his father’s glory,
although it has not undergone any change.

Espa├▒ol

Nuevamente, cuando el Pr├нncipe est├б en la prisi├│n, es desagradable.
Pero cuando el emperador se complace en liberarlo
y colocarlo a su lado para disfrutar de las placeres como ├йl
La casa de la prisi├│n puede parecer agradable
Como s├нmbolo de la gloria de su padre,
aunque no ha sufrido ning├║n cambio.

English

In Tiruvoymozi 4-8 it is said :-

“As the Lord does not care for me,
it would not at all matter if I lost all that I would otherwise prize highly,
viz., my beauty, my mind, my modesty, the sheen of my complexion, my intelligence, my charm, my bracelets, my girdle, my body and my very life.”

Espa├▒ol

En Tiruvoymozi 4-8 se dice:-

“Como el Se├▒or no me importa,
No importar├нa en absoluto si perdiera todo lo que de otra manera premiar├нa,
a saber - mi belleza, mi mente, mi modestia, el brillo de mi tez, mi inteligencia, mi encanto, mis pulseras, mi faja, mi cuerpo y mi propia vida “.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рд╕рдВрд╢реНрд▓реЗрд╖-рд░рд╛рд╣рд┐рддреНрдпреЗрди рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрдп рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐-рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ

рдореБрдХреНрддрдВ рд╕рдВрдкрдиреНрдирдВ рдирд┐рд░рддрд┐рд╢рдп-рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЕрдиреБрднрд╡рдВ рдХреБрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдгрдВ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐
рдирд┐рд░рддрд┐рд╢рдп-рднреЛрдЧреНрдп-рд╡рд░реНрдЧреЗ рд╜рдиреНрддрд░реНрднрд╛рд╡рдГ рдЙрдкрдкрдиреНрдирдГ ред

English

As illustrated in the passages cited above,
the objects of this world (L─лl─Б Vibh┼лti),
which appear disagreeable or only slightly agreeable,
when the j─лva is not blessed with union with the Lord,

may appear supremely agreeable,
when he has become a mukta enjoying without intermission (the bliss of) Bhagav─Бn.

Espa├▒ol

Como se ilustra en los pasajes citados anteriormente,
Los objetos de este mundo (l─лl─Б vibh┼лti),
que parecen desagradables o solo un poco agradables,
Cuando el J─лva no es bendecido con la uni├│n con el Se├▒or,

puede parecer supremamente agradable,
Cuando se ha convertido en un Mukta disfrutando sin intermedio (la dicha de) Bhagav─Бn.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЗрддреНрдердВ рдмрджреНрдзрд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рддрд┐
рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдХреВрд▓рддрдпрд╛ рд╜рд▓реНрдкрд╛рдиреБрдХреВрд▓рддрдпрд╛,
рдХрд░реНрдо-рдмрдиреНрдз-рд░рд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рддрд┐ рдЕрдиреБрдХреВрд▓-рд╕реНрд╡рднрд╛рд╡рддрдпрд╛ рдЪ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐рд╕реН
рддреЗрд╖рд╛рдВ рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдирд╛рдВ рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЗрдЪреНрдЫрд╛рджрд┐-рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрд╛ред

English

There is nothing inconsistent in this.
The same object may be disagreeable
or only slightly agreeable
to a man bound to saс╣Бs─Бra,

while to one released from the bondage of karma,
it is agreeable.
This is the nature ordained for them by the will of God.

Espa├▒ol

No hay nada inconsistente en esto.
El mismo objeto puede ser desagradable
o solo un poco agradable
a un hombre unido a Saс╣Бs─Бra,

mientras que a uno liber├│ de la esclavitud del karma,
Es agradable.

Esta es la naturaleza ordenada para ellos
por la voluntad de Dios.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

who has, for his prak─Бra or mode, all things whose agreeableness is dependent on His will,

is implicit in the words in the dative or fourth case (N─Бr─Бyaс╣З─Бya) in Tirumantra and in Dvaya.

рдкреБрдгреНрдп-рдкрд╛рдк-рдХрд░реНрдо-рдирд┐рд░рдкреЗрдХреНрд╖–рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЗрдЪреНрдЫрд╛рдиреБрдЧреБрдг–рд╕реНрд╡реЗрдЪреНрдЫрд╛-рдореВрд▓рдХрддреНрд╡рд╛рджреН

English

( It is said in the ┼Ыrutis that the mukta eats whatever he wants
and can create whichever relations he wants).
The enjoyment of food in the state of mukti
and the contact with relations and the like
are not due to karma, whether puс╣Зya or papa,
but are dependent only on the will of the mukta
which is (always ) in accordance with the will of Bhagav─Бn.

Therefore they are not the consequences or fruits of karma,
but fall into the category of pure service
which is the overflow of the perfect enjoyment of Brahman.

Espa├▒ol

(Se dice en el ┼Ъrutis que el Mukta
come lo que quiera
y puede crear las relaciones que desee).
El disfrute de la comida en el estado de Mukti
y el contacto con las relaciones y similares
no se deben al karma, ya sea Puс╣Зya o pap├б,
pero solo dependen de la voluntad del mukta
que es (siempre) de acuerdo con la voluntad de Bhagav─Бn.

Por lo tanto, no son las consecuencias o frutos del karma,
pero cae en la categor├нa de servicio puro
que es el desbordamiento del disfrute perfecto de Brahman.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдпрд╛рдиреНрддрд░реНрдЧрдд–рд╕реНрд╡-рдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрдж–рд╡рд┐рд╣рд╛рд░реЗрдг

English

Even if they come to L─лl─Б-vibh┼лti (this world of ours) by their own will and pleasure
which are of the form of service to the Lord,
there will be no diminution of their enjoyment of Brahman
and in this sense there will be no return to saс╣Бs─Бra.

que son de la forma de servicio al Se├▒or,
No habr├б disminuci├│n de su disfrute de Brahman y en este sentido no habr├б retorno a Saс╣Бs─Бra.

in the state of the quest for mukti
and maintain that, in accordance with these degrees of merit or demerit (while in the state of seeking mukti),
there would be differences in enjoyment
even after they have attained mukti.

Some hold that,
in accordance with defects in the observance of the prescribed code of conduct by the seeker after mukti, there would be diminution in the bliss enjoyed.

Even admitting that their words deserve serious consideration
as those of trust worthy authorities,
they mean only this much that,
in the enjoyment of Bhagav─Бn which occurs before mukti,
there would be degrees of joy.

Espa├▒ol

Algunos sostienen eso,
De acuerdo con los defectos en la observancia del c├│digo de conducta
prescrito por el buscador despu├йs de Mukti,
habr├нa disminuci├│n en la dicha disfrutada.

Incluso admitiendo que sus palabras merecen una consideraci├│n seria
Como los de las autoridades dignas de la confianza,
Significan solo tanto que,
En el disfrute de Bhagav─Бn que ocurre antes de Mukti,
Habr├нa grados de alegr├нa.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдкрд╢реНрдЪрд╛рдиреН рдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдирд╛рдВ (рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдореН рдЕрдирдиреБрднрд╡рд╛рддреН) рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ рдиреНрдпреВрдирддрд╛-рдорд╛рддреНрд░рдореН,
рди рддреНрд╡реН рдЕрд░реНрде-рдиреНрдпреВрдирддрд╛ ред

English

It is true that there may be delay or no delay in attaining release from bondage,
but after release is (once) attained,
there is no difference at all in the enjoyment of bliss (between muktas and muktas).

Espa├▒ol

Es cierto que puede haber retraso o ning├║n retraso para obtener la liberaci├│n de la esclavitud,
Pero despu├йs del lanzamiento se alcanza (una vez),
No hay ninguna diferencia en el disfrute de la dicha (entre Muktas y Muktas).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рд╢реНрд░реА-рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреБ-рд▓реЛрдХрд╛рджрд┐рд╖реБ рд╕рд╛рд▓реЛрдХреНрдп-рд╕рд╛рд░реВрдкреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐-рдорд╛рддреНрд░рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд╡рддрд╛рдВ

English

Some j─лvas attain, in such worlds as those of Viс╣гс╣Зu,
the privilege of living in the same world as Viс╣гс╣Зu (s─Бlokya ),
some j─лvas attain proximity to the presence of Viс╣гс╣Зu (s─Бmipya );
some attain forms similar to that of Viс╣гс╣Зu (s─Бr┼лpya):
these, too, are sometimes called muktas by courtesy (upac─Бra),
since they are very near the ultimate goal
(but they are not really muktas in the true sense of the word).

Espa├▒ol

Algunos J─лvas alcanzan, en mundos como los de Viс╣гс╣Зu,
El privilegio de vivir en el mismo mundo que Viс╣гс╣Зu (S─Бlokya),
Algunos J─лvas alcanzan la proximidad a la presencia de Viс╣гс╣Зu (S─Бmipya);
Algunos alcanzan formas similares a las de Viс╣гс╣Зu (S─Бr┼лpya):
Estos tambi├йn a veces se llaman muktas por cortes├нa (upac─Бra),
ya que est├бn muy cerca del objetivo final
(Pero en realidad no son muktas en el verdadero sentido de la palabra).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрдпрдореН рдЕрд░реНрдердГ

тАШтАШрд▓реЛрдХреЗрд╖реБ рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреЛрд░реН рдирд┐рд╡рд╕рдиреНрддрд┐ рдХреЗрдЪрд┐рддреН
рд╕рдореАрдкрдореН рдЛрдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрддрд┐ рдЪ рдХреЗрдЪрд┐рджреН рдЕрдиреНрдпреЗ ред
рдЕрдиреНрдпреЗ рддреБ рд░реВрдкрдВ рд╕рджреГрд╢рдВ рднрдЬрдиреНрддреЗ
рд╕рд╛рдпреБрдЬреНрдпрдореН рдЕрдиреНрдпреЗ рд╕ рддреБ рдореЛрдХреНрд╖ рдЙрдХреНрддрдГ +++(рдирд╛рдиреНрдпрддреН)+++реетАЩтАЩ
(рд╢реНрд░реАрднрд╛рдЧрд╡рддрдореН )

рдЗрддрд┐ рдирд┐рдпрдордирд╛рддреН рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрдГ рее

English

This idea is set forth in the following ┼Ыloka -

“Some live in the worlds of Viс╣гс╣Зu ;
others approach very near to Viс╣гс╣Зu ;
others, again, acquire forms resembling Viс╣гс╣Зu’s;
yet others attain sayujya with Viс╣гс╣Зu .
This, alone, is called mokс╣гa .”

Espa├▒ol

Esta idea se establece en el siguiente ┼Ъloka -

“Algunos viven en los mundos de Viс╣гс╣Зu;
Otros se acercan muy cerca de Viс╣гс╣Зu;
Otros, nuevamente, adquieren formas que se asemejan a las de Viс╣гс╣Зu;
Sin embargo, otros alcanzan Sayujya con Viс╣гс╣Зu.
Esto, solo, se llama mokс╣гa “.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

In the same way as a hundred and the like are included within a thousand,

El Mukta se llama Sayuk (con Brahman).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдПрд╡рдВ рд╕рддрд┐
рд╢реНрд░реБрддреМ рд╕рд╛рдпреБрдЬреНрдп-рд╢рдмреНрджрд╕реНрдп рд╕рд╛рд╖реНрд░реНрд╖реНрдЯрд┐рддрд╛-рд╢рдмреНрджрд╕реНрдп рдЪ рд╕рд╣ рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЧрдГ рдХреБрдд

рдЗрддрд┐ рдЪреЗрддреН тАФ

English

In this connection, it may be asked

why, in one of the passages of the Veda, the two words, sayujya and s─Бrshtitha are employed (in the same sentence ),
when they mean the same thing,
namely, communion in the enjoyment
(would it not be redundant to use two words when one would be enough?).

Espa├▒ol

A este respecto, se puede preguntar

Por qu├й, en uno de los pasajes del Veda, se emplean las dos palabras, Sayujya y S─Бrshtitha (en la misma oraci├│n),
Cuando significan lo mismo,
a saber, comuni├│n en el disfrute
(┬┐No ser├нa redundante usar dos palabras cuando una ser├нa suficiente?).

рддрд╛рд░-рддрдореНрдп-рд╡рд┐рд╣реАрдирддрд╛ рее+++(4)+++

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рд╕рд╛рдпреБрдЬреНрдпрдореН рдЙрднрдпреЛрд░реН рдЕрддреНрд░
рднреЛрдХреНрддрд╡реНрдпрд╕реНрдпрд╛рд╡рд┐рд╢рд┐рд╖реНрдЯрддрд╛ ред
рд╕рд╛рд░реНрд╖реНрдЯрд┐рддрд╛ рддрддреНрд░ рднреЛрдЧрд╕реНрдп
рддрд╛рд░-рддрдореНрдп-рд╡рд┐рд╣реАрдирддрд╛ рее+++(4)+++

English

The answer is (that there is a difference in meaning between the two words ),
and it is as follows:

Sayujyam between the two (Brahman and the mukta) means that
there is no difference
so far as the objects of enjoyment are concerned.
s─Бrshtita (between the two) means that
there is no difference
in the degree or intensity of their enjoyment.
(Two men may have before them the same object of enjoyment
and yet one of them may enjoy it more intensely than the other).

Espa├▒ol

La respuesta es (que hay una diferencia en el significado entre las dos palabras),
Y es como sigue:

Sayujyam entre los dos (Brahman y Mukta) significa que No hay diferencia
En lo que respecta a los objetos de disfrute.

s─Бrshtita (entre los dos) significa que
No hay diferencia
en el grado o intensidad de su disfrute.

(Dos hombres pueden tener ante ellos el mismo objeto de disfrute
Y, sin embargo, uno de ellos puede disfrutarlo m├бs intensamente que el otro).

To those (viz. Advaitins) who maintain that the word Sayujyam means oneness or identity with Brahman (aikyam),
the derivative or etymological meaning of the word, s├гyujyam,
is at variance, as also the texts in the ┼Ыruti which declare that Brahman is different from the j─лvas.

[ Such ┼Ыrutis as the following:-
Brahman is the eternal among eternals,
the sentient among sentients.
(1) He is one and satisfies the desires of the many:
Svetasvatara Upaniс╣гad.
(2) Without any blemish or stain
he attains perfect resemblance (paramam samyam).]

Besides, their view is opposed also to the ┼Ыrutis
which declare that the mukta will attain perfect resemblance (s─Бmyam) to Brahman
and that the mukta will be like Brahman.

  • Brahman es el eterno entre los eternos, el sensible entre los sentientes.
  • ├Йl es uno y satisface los deseos de los muchos: Svetasvatara Upaniс╣гad.
  • sin mancha ni mancha
    ├Йl alcanza la semejanza perfecta (Paramam samyam).]

Adem├бs, su punto de vista se opone tambi├йn al ┼Ъrutis
que declara que el Mukta obtendr├б un parecido perfecto (S─Бmyam) con Brahman

English

“The j─лva released from bondage (i.e.) the mukta,
attains the Supreme Being
and acquires attributes similar to those of the Supreme Being.
He too becomes free from all imperfections when he reaches Him.
Having attained the Omniscient Brahman, he, too, becomes omniscient.

alcanza el ser supremo

├Йl tambi├йn se libera de todas las imperfecciones cuando lo alcanza.
Habiendo alcanzado el omnisciente Brahman, ├йl tambi├йn se vuelve omnisciente.

English

Thus since in the ┼Ыrutis, the smс╣Ыtis and the s┼лtras,
resemblance between the mukta and Brahman (s─Бmyam) is explicitly stated,
those places in the texts which seem to speak of identity (aikyam) between the mukta and Brahman in the state of release from bondage
have to be explained in a manner that would not be inconsistent
with the ┼Ыruti s which declare difference between the j─лva and Brahman.
The word aikyam or (identity ) in such passages
should be construed in the same manner as in the ┼Ыloka : >

“The aikyam between R─Бma and Sugr─лva arose O, Lady, in this way.тАЭ
(Here aikyam means friendship, identity not of selfs but of interests).

Espa├▒ol

As├н, ya que en los ┼Ыrutis, los smс╣Ыtis y los s┼лtras,
La semejanza entre Mukta y Brahman (S─Бmyam) se afirma expl├нcitamente,
Esos lugares en los textos que parecen hablar de identidad (aikyam) entre Mukta y Brahman en el estado de liberaci├│n de la esclavitud
tener que ser explicado de una manera que no ser├нa inconsistente
con los ┼Ъrutis que declaran la diferencia entre J─лva y Brahman.

La palabra aikyam o (identidad) en tales pasajes
debe interpretarse de la misma manera que en el ┼Ъloka:

“El aikyam entre R─Бma y Sugr─лva surgi├│ O, dama, de esta manera”.
(Aqu├н Aikyam significa amistad,
identidad no de s├н mismo, sino de intereses).

English

If it were not construed in this way,

(1) тАЬWhen the person who is twice-born (dvija) sees that he is different from the Supreme Being
and that the Supreme Being is different from himself,
he becomes free from bondage
and will see for ever (Bhagav─Бn who is) the 26th real.

Espa├▒ol

Si no se interpret├│ de esta manera,

(1) тАЬCuando la persona que tiene dos veces (dvija) ve que es diferente del ser supremo
y que el ser supremo es diferente de s├н mismo,
se libera de la esclavitud
y ver├й para siempre (bhagav─Бn que es) el 26 de verdad.

English

English

The Supreme Being, O, king, is different from the j─лva,
and the j─лva, who is the 25th real, is different from the 24 reals.
Therefore good men do not consider the j─лva,
who is the 25th real,
as being identical with the Supreme Being.

Espa├▒ol

Y el J─лva, que es el 25 real, es diferente de los 24 reales.
Por lo tanto, los hombres buenos no consideran el J─лva,
Quien es el 25 en realidad
como es id├йntico al ser supremo.

(4) “Just as fire in a ball of (red-hot) iron seems to be one with the iron,
though it is really different from it,
so the Supreme Being pervades the world

I┼Ыvara has, for His definition, the following attributes which are like the umbrella and the chamara (insignia of royalty):–

  • being the cause of the world,
  • the conferring of mokс╣гa on j─лvas,
  • being the support of the world,
  • being the controller of the world,
  • the one for whom all things and all sentient beings exist, the one who has everything for His body,
  • the one who is denoted by all words,
  • the one who can be understood from all the Vedas,
  • the one who is the refuge of all the world,
  • the one who should be adored by all those who want mokс╣гa ,
  • the one who grants the fruits (of all actions),
  • the one whose essential nature is omnipresence, J├▒─Бna and ─Бnanda (bliss),
  • the one who is the spouse of Lakс╣гmi.

These are peculiar to Him and are His distinctive features.

рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╖реНрдард┐рддрдВ рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрдореН ред

English

Ever in the state of desire for mukti,
the mukta had an aversion to the enjoyment of non-sentient things (matter)
and also to the mere enjoyment of his own self (kaivalya).
This aversion is now well established in him;
for as he sees all things having Brahman as their inner self,
there is no possibility of his enjoying his own self as separate (from everything else),
and as he sees by constant perception (pratyakс╣гa ) the imperfections of all other objects (than God).

Espa├▒ol

Alguna vez en el estado de deseo de Mukti,
El Mukta ten├нa una aversi├│n al disfrute de las cosas no sintientes (materia)
y tambi├йn al mero disfrute de su propio ser (Kaivalya).

Esta aversi├│n ahora est├б bien establecida en ├йl; porque como ve todas las cosas teniendo a Brahman como su ser interno,
No hay posibilidad de que disfrute de s├н mismo como separado (de todo lo dem├бs),
y como ve por percepci├│n constante (pratyakс╣гa) las imperfecciones de todos los dem├бs objetos (que Dios).

English

The knowledge which formerly in saс╣Бs─Бra deepened into the form of love called bhakti
and which he acquired by his distinctive knowledge of the specific nature of Bhagav─Бn
has, now, in the state of mukti, become ripened into the form of supreme love,
because he has now a vision of all aspects of Bhagav─Бn’s distinctive nature of which even the ┼Ы─Бstra-s are incapable.

Espa├▒ol

El conocimiento que anteriormente en Saс╣Бs─Бra se profundiz├│ en la forma de amor llamado Bhakti
y que adquiri├│ por su conocimiento distintivo de la naturaleza espec├нfica de Bhagav─Бn

Se ha madurado, ahora, en el estado de Mukti, en forma de amor supremo,
Porque ahora tiene una visi├│n de todos los aspectos de la naturaleza distintiva de Bhagav─Бn de la cual incluso los ┼Ъ─Бstra-s son incapaces.

English

Therefore I┼Ыvara’s great love for him
as stated in the ┼Ыloka :

“The jnan─л is dear to me
(How dear he is to me
cannot be described even by me,
Omniscient though I am)”

I┼Ыvara’s love for him is so overwhelming
that its flow is irresistible
and that its current reaches even those uplands
which are connected with him only in distant relationship.

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, el gran amor de I┼Ыvara por ├йl
Como se indica en el ┼Ъloka:

“El Jnan─л es querido para m├н
(Que querido es para mi
no puede ser descrito ni siquiera por m├н,
Omnisciente aunque soy) "

El amor de I┼Ыvara por ├йl es tan abrumador
que su flujo es irresistible
y que su corriente llega incluso a esas tierras altas
que est├бn conectados con ├йl solo en una relaci├│n lejana.

English

Therefore it cannot be stated that,
though he is free from karma,
there is the possibility of his returning to saс╣Бs─Бra by the will of I┼Ыvara
who is independent (and all-powerful).

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, no se puede afirmar que,
Aunque est├б libre de karma,
Existe la posibilidad de que regrese a Saс╣Бs─Бra por la voluntad de I┼Ыvara
quien es independiente (y todo-poderoso).

(i.e.) it will last as long as his soul lasts.

Espa├▒ol

рдкрд░рд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрдирдореН рдЕрдиреНрддрд░рд╛ рдкреНрд░реАрддреНрдпрд╛ рд╡рд░реНрд╖рдорд╛рдиреЗ рднреЛрдЧреЗ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╖реНрдард┐рддрд╛ рднрд╡реЗрдоред

English

Having reached the dazzling region of Paramapada
and approached the Lord crowned with fragrant tulas─л,
who is ever delighted in doing what is good to all beings,
and having obtained our share in service (to them),
we shall ever live under the sounding anklets of the assembly of our ─Бc─Бryas
and enjoy delights which will never change
and which will spring (from within us) to our great joy.

Espa├▒ol

Habiendo llegado a la deslumbrante regi├│n de Paramapada
y se acerc├│ al Se├▒or coronado con fragantes tulas─л,
quien siempre est├б encantado de hacer lo bueno para todos los seres,
y habiendo obtenido nuestra participaci├│n en el servicio (para ellos),
alguna vez viviremos debajo de las tobilleras de la asamblea de nuestros ─Бc─Бryas
y disfrutamos de las delicias que nunca cambiar├бn
y que surgir├б (desde dentro de nosotros) hasta nuestra gran alegr├нa.

рдЕрд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд░рд╛рдиреНрдд-рд╢реНрд░рджреНрдзрд╛+++(тЖТрдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдп-рдЪрд┐рдХреАрд░реНрд╖рд╛)+++-рд╢рдд-рдХрд▓рд╣-рдХрд▓реНрд▓реЛрд▓-рдХрд▓реБрд╖рд╛

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд░рд╛рдиреНрдд-рд╢реНрд░рджреНрдзрд╛+++(тЖТрдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдп-рдЪрд┐рдХреАрд░реНрд╖рд╛)+++-рд╢рдд-рдХрд▓рд╣-рдХрд▓реНрд▓реЛрд▓-рдХрд▓реБрд╖рд╛

рдордзреБ-рдХреНрд╖реАрд░-рдиреНрдпрд╛рдп–рд╕реНрд╡-рдЧреБрдг–рд╡рд┐рднрд╡рд╛рд╕рдЮреНрдЬрди+++(=рд╕рдВрдпреЛрдЧ)+++–рдХрдирдиреН+++(тЖРрджреАрдкреНрддрд┐-рдХрд╛рдиреНрддрд┐-рдЧрддрд┐рд╖реБ)+++-
рдорд╣рд╛рдирдиреНрдж-рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рдиреБрднрд╡-рдкрд░рд┐рд╡рд╛рд╣рд╛ рдмрд╣реБ-рд╡рд┐рдзрд╛рдГ рее рекреп рее

English

May Varied forms of service
which are the overflow of the blissful enjoyment of Brahma
arising from the greatness of His qualities and glorious possessions
which are blended together like honey and milk -
may these forms of service
in which there is a conflict of hundreds of unwearied desires (to render service ) and which are easy of attainment for such as seers and s┼лris -
may these manifest themselves in my mind!

Espa├▒ol

Variadas formas de servicio
que son el desbordamiento del disfrute feliz de Brahma
surgiendo de la grandeza de sus cualidades y posesiones gloriosas
que se mezclan como la miel y la leche -
Que estas formas de servicio
en el que hay un conflicto de cientos de deseos inseguros (para prestar el servicio)
y que son f├бciles de lograr para los videntes y S┼лris,
┬бque se manifiesten en mi mente!

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдЯрд┐рдкреНрдкрдиреА

рдЕрддреНрд░реИрддрджреН-рдЧреНрд░рдиреНрдердЧрдд-рдирд╛рдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░-рд╕реВрдЪрдирд╛ рд╜рд╕реНрддрд┐ред

English

Having received the gracious look of the Lord (and of the ─Аc─Бrya)
and understood what is most essential and most important in the ┼Ы─Бstras (vis, the three mantras or rahasyas),
having obtained a clear and accurate knowledge of his own self and of the Supreme Being
and conquered his attachment to other interests in life,
having acquired a knowledge of what is appropriate for the different kinds of adhik─Бr─лs,
and realised the nature of the two up─Бyas (bhakti and prapatti),
having become troubled (in mind) (at his inability to adopt other up─Бyas)
and performed bharany─Бsa with all its aс╣Еgas
and thus done what he ought to do,
performing here in this world the adoration of the Lord (and His devotees )
without faults and in accordance with his state or niс╣гс╣нh─Б
and in the manner prescribed in the ┼Ы─Бstras
and having (thereafter) cast off (both ) the gross (sth┼лla) and subtle prakс╣Ыti (body),
some one there may be who enjoys Bhagav─Бn eternally.

(This ┼Ыloka refers concisely to the gist of each of the twenty two chapters in the first part of the treatise.)

Espa├▒ol

Habiendo recibido el aspecto amable del Se├▒or (y del ─Бc─Бrya)
y entendi├│ lo que es m├бs esencial y m├бs importante en los ┼Ы─Бstras (vis, los tres mantras o rahasyas),
habiendo obtenido un conocimiento claro y preciso de su propio ser y del ser supremo
y conquist├│ su apego a otros intereses de la vida,
habiendo adquirido un conocimiento de lo que es apropiado para los diferentes tipos de adhik─Бr─лs,
y se dio cuenta de la naturaleza de los dos up─Бyas (Bhakti y Prapatti),
haberse preocupado (en mente) (por su incapacidad para adoptar otros up─Бyas)
y realiz├│ bharany─Бsa con todas sus aс╣Еgas
y as├н hizo lo que deber├нa hacer,
actuando aqu├н en este mundo la adoraci├│n del Se├▒or (y sus devotos)
sin fallas y de acuerdo con su estado o niс╣гс╣нh─Б
y de la manera prescrita en los ┼Ъ─Бstras
y que (a partir de entonces) cayera (ambos) el bruto (sth┼лla) y sutil prakс╣Ыti (cuerpo),
Alguien puede ser que disfrute de Bhagav─Бn eternamente.

(Esto ┼Ъloka se refiere concisamente a la esencia de cada uno de los veintid├│s cap├нtulos
en la primera parte del tratado).

рдЗрдЩреНрдЧреБ рдкрд┐рд░рд┐рдХрд░рд╢рдмреНрджрддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ рдкрд░рд┐рдХрд░рд╡рд┐рднрд╛рдЧрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердВ , рднрд░рдиреНрдпрд╛рд╕рд╢рдмреНрджрддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ рд╕рд╛рдЩрдЧрдкреНрд░рдкрджрдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН , рдирд┐рд╖реНрдкрдиреНрдирдХреГрддрдпрд╢рдмреНрджрддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ рдХреГрддрдХреГрддреНрдпрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН рд╕реВрдЪрд┐рддрдЩреНрдЧрд│реНред рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рд╡рд╕реНрдерд╛рд░реНрд╣рдВ тАУ рд╕реНрд╡рд░реВрдкреЛрдкрд╛рдпрдкреБрд░реБрд╖рд╛рд░реНрдердирд┐рд╖реНрдард╛рднрд┐рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд░реВрдкрдорд╛рдй рддрдйреНрдйреБрдбреИрдп рджрд╢реИрдХреНрдиреБрдЧреБрдгрдорд╛рдЧред рдЗрджрдйрд╛рд▓реН рд╕реНрд╡рдирд┐рд╖реНрдард╛рднрд┐рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдерд╕реНрд╕рдЩреНрдЧреГрд╣реАрддрдГ ред рд╕рдкрд░реНрдпрд╛рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдореЖрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рдЙрддреНрддрд░рдХреГрддреНрдпрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН, рд╕рдкрд░реНрдпреИрдХреНрдХреБ рдХрд╛рд╖реНрдард╛рднреВрддрдорд╛рдй рднрд╛рдЧрд╡рддрдХреИрдЩрдХрд░реНрдпрддреНрддрд┐рдйреН рдорд╛рд╣рд╛рддреНрдореНрдпрдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдкрд╛рджрдХрдорд╛рдй рдкреБрд░реБрд╖рд╛рд░реНрдерддрдХрд╛рд╖реНрдард╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН рд╕реВрдЪрд┐рддрдореНред
рдЗрд╣ рдирд┐рдпрддрдореЖрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░реАрдпрдирд┐рдпрдордирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдЧрд╕рдореЖрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рдЕрдкрд░рд╛рдзрдкрд░рд┐рд╣рд╛рд░рд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН,
рдХрд╛рдкрд┐ рдмрд┐рднреНрд░рддреН рдОрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН, рдирд┐рд░реНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╕реНрдереВрд▓рд╕реВрдХреНрд╖реНрдордкреНрд░рдХреГрддрд┐рдГ рдОрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рдирд┐рд░реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН рдЧрддрд┐рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддрдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореБрдореН рд╕реВрдЪрд┐рдкреНрдкрд┐рдХреНрдХрдмрдЯреНрдЯрджреБрдЧрд│реНред
рдЕрдЪреНрдпреБрддрдВ рдирд┐рддреНрдпрдордиреБрднрд╡рддрд┐рдОрдйреНрдмрджрд╛рд▓реН рдкрд░рд┐рдкреВрд░реНрдгрдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рдиреБрднрд╡рд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореН рд╕реВрдЪрд┐рддрдореНред

  1. Namo Bhagavate Vasudevaya: with Om (or aum) preceding it. ↩︎
